      As for the service, except for the doorman who is quite smart, the others really have not received any training. The staff wear slippers and walk in the lobby. No one greets the cleaning staff or other staff in the hotel.
      Because I stayed for several consecutive days and had to change rooms on the last day, I placed separate orders and explained the situation to the front desk in advance. However, when I checked in, the front desk was extremely unprofessional. After waiting for more than ten minutes, I finally found the order and finally gave When I received the room card, I didn't mention changing rooms on the last day. After taking the initiative to ask, I checked for a long time and was told that I could handle it at the front desk on the last day. There was no mention of breakfast time, where the breakfast room was, the opening hours of the gym, etc., but I still took the initiative to ask. It was very late when I checked in, and there was no one waiting to check in. The front desk was not in a hurry.
      On the last day, I was anxious to catch a flight and had to leave at 7:30. I didn't have time to go to the breakfast restaurant (meals open at 7), so I called the front desk to ask if they could send breakfast to the room. Without any hesitation, the front desk told me that breakfast must be eaten directly in the restaurant and cannot be delivered. I have stayed in many hotels, whether they are five-star hotels or express hotels, and I have never encountered one where food delivery was not possible. msg:When I came to Haikou, I was torn between Langham, Sofitel, and Hilton. I finally chose Langham. Now I don‚Äôt regret it too much. This Langham is really toxic.

The reason I chose Langham is simple. My impression of other Langhams is much better than Sofitel and Hilton, and it looks really good in the photos. Although The Langham is not a top five-star hotel brand in the world, I have stayed in quite a few. When I went to Hong Kong as a child, I basically stayed at the Langham Hotel in Hong Kong. I also stayed at the Langham Donghai Hotel in Shenzhen many times. I even stayed at the Langham in Los Angeles. But this Langham is the worst of all the Langhams I have stayed at so far. Except that the decoration style of this Langham hotel is very similar to Langham, it does not meet Langham standards at all.

Let‚Äôs talk about service first. I recognize the professionalism of this hotel's service, but overall it's really unsatisfactory. Let me talk about the concierge first. He gave people a very "lazy" feeling. He opened the car door and left without even saying hello. The concierge is the first employee that guests meet when they arrive at the hotel. As a result, he doesn't even bother to say "good afternoon". It's not just any concierge, it's almost every concierge. Let‚Äôs talk about cleaning. As soon as I entered the room, I found a large core under the bedside table, similar to the core of a jackfruit. This is really a lonely place to check. You said it would be fine if you didn't find the watermelon seeds. Can't you even see such a big core? Then there is the daily cleaning work, which is really lazy to the extreme. The tea cup was not returned to its original position in the minibar, and the hair dryer was not returned to its previous drawer. Taking tips from us is 100 times more positive than doing the work. And this mineral water, only two bottles, is too expensive. Although you can call for mineral water in most hotels, but how many customers would have the audacity to call and ask for a few dollars of mineral water? Let‚Äôs talk about the breakfast. It‚Äôs really one of the worst breakfasts in any five-star hotel I‚Äôve stayed at this year. There is never anyone to guide you to your seat when you enter the restaurant, and you even have to pour tea yourself. The most outrageous thing was on the last day, when the breakfast receptionist saw me, he said two words: room number. Have such employees received training? Can't you even say a basic "Good morning sir, which room are you staying in?" Then we sat down and didn't even help set the tableware. I could only find a table with tableware and bring the tableware to our table. Let‚Äôs talk about the front desk. It is very professional and has the characteristic of giving every lady a flower. His Mandarin is also very standard. I feel that the front desk of your hotel is not like a hotel like other departments. I hope you can reflect on it.

As for the facilities, I can only say that the person who designed this room was either drunk or ****. Why do you think the minibar should not be placed on the wall but in the center of the room? What a hindrance, the whole room feels much smaller. If the reason is that there is a mirror on the wall, then why do you have to put a mirror there? And that toilet door. I never thought that I would stay in a five-star hotel and the toilet door would be broken. You must open the door gently with both hands. You can't open it with one hand; you can't open it with too much force. It took me nearly ten minutes to open this door the first time. Can't you just design a simple sliding door for a toilet? It has to be so complicated. This kind of problem that only occurs in all seasons should not appear in a high-end hotel. Again, it‚Äôs a good thing, but it‚Äôs useless. Let‚Äôs talk about the socket. The two sockets at the bedside often had poor contact, and one of my mother's newly purchased charging cables was damaged. And the Wi-Fi connection drops every minute or two even when I'm lying in bed.

All in all, this Langham almost shattered all my good impressions of this brand. Don‚Äôt be fooled by his photos, because apart from the decoration style and the pink taxi at the door, he is completely unworthy of the name Langham. Just stay at Sofitel and Hilton.

The second is service. Langham's service intentions are surprising and moving. Please indicate your birthday when booking, upgrade the room, and give you an executive afternoon tea. The cake given to Westin in Xiamen last year was very perfunctory and could only be photographed. The W Hotel in Xi'an also gave a symbolic bottle of red wine when checking out. All in all it is recommended to stay.
